postSubroutineBegin: s32'CPUEstimate'
  if: Mem(EXBoss)
    callSubroutine: s32'EX_Estimate'
  endIf: 
  else: 
    callSubroutine: s32'Boss_Estimate'
  endElse: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'Boss_Estimate'
  ifNot: Mem(IsEnemyDamage)
    skillLowEstimation: s32'SacredEdge'
    skillLowEstimation: s32'RideTheLightning'
    skillLowEstimation: s32'AirRideTheLightning'
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(Tension), Val(5000)
      skillLowEstimation: s32'NmlAtk5E'
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(1000000)
      callSubroutine: s32'FarSealAtk'
      ifTrueInObject: (ENEMY), Mem(IsLand)
        skillHighEstimation: s32'StunEdge1'
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    else:

beginSubroutine: s32'NmlTaidenAdd'
  upon: (HIT)
    ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal0)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
      createObject: s32'Taiden_Effect', (ENEMY_CENTER)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(180)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(180)
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  upon: (ENEMY_GUARD)
    ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal0)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
      createObject: s32'Taiden_Effect', (ENEMY_CENTER)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(180)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(180)
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'KYKBOSS_DustAttack'
  createObject: s32'cmn_Dust_alarm', (PLAYER)
  callSubroutine: s32'cmn_AtkLv2'
  dustAttack: 1
  guardType: (HIGH)
  damage: Val(40)
  riscConsumeStarter: 20
  setProration: 80
  hitAirPushbackX: Val(50000)
  hitAirPushbackY: Val(30000)
  groundHitEffect: (AIR_FACE_UP)
  airHitEffect: (AIR_FACE_UP)
  hitStop: 20
  enemyHitstopAddition: 0, 0, 0
  atkAngle: 45
  pushbackX: 60
  callSubroutine: s32'cmn_fuwafuwafuwa'
  hitAirPushbackX: Val(10000)
  hitAirPushbackXOverTime: Val(80), Val(6), Val(10)
  hitAirPushbackY: Val(30000)
  hitAirPushbackYOverTime: Val(60), Val(8), Val(16)
  hitGravity: Val(500)
  hitGravityOverTime: Val(250), Val(5), Val(30)
  attackExHitParam: Val(700), 0, 10000, 1, (ENEMY), Mem(WSBPoint)
  hitSoundEffect: s32'SE_BTL_CMN_Hit_Grap_L'
  guardSoundEffect: s32'SE_BTL_CMN_Guard_Grap_L'
  enableSpecialCancel: 0
  enableOverdriveCancel: 0
  deactivateObjectByName: s32'cmn_Dust_Camera_POV'
  deactivateObjectByName: s32'cmn_Dust_Camera_POG'
  deactivateObjectByName: s32'cmn_Dust_Speed'
  deactivateObjectByName: s32'cmn_Dust_CenterLine'
  deactivateObjectByName: s32'cmn_Dust_SpeedLine'
  deactivateObjectByName: s32'cmn_Dust_TailSmoke'
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Val(320000), Mem(FuncArg0), Mem(ActReg0)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Val(100000), Mem(FuncArg1), Mem(ActReg1)
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (ADD), Val(100000), Mem(FuncArg2), Mem(ActReg2)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg7), Val(1)
  upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
    checkInput: (INPUT_HOLD_D)
    ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg7), Val(0)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(28)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg7), Val(1)
      attackLevel: 4
      damagePercent: 125
      createObject: s32'cmn_hit_chargedust', (CENTER)
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  upon: (ENEMY_GUARD)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (ENEMY_GUARD)
    if: Mem(ActReg7)
      blockstunAmount: 18
      riscGain: 25
      pushbackX: 100
    endIf: 
    ifNot: Mem(EXBoss)
      ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal0)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
        createObject: s32'Taiden_Effect', (ENEMY_CENTER)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(180)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(180)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  upon: (HIT)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (HIT)
    if: Mem(ActReg7)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK_GROUNDED)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (COUNTER_HIT)
      checkMoveFlag: (ENEMY_IN_HITSTUN)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      checkCurrentStateName: (ENEMY), s32'CmnActHajikareStand'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(0)
      endIf: 
      checkCurrentStateName: (ENEMY), s32'CmnActHajikareCrouch'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(0)
      endIf: 
      checkCurrentStateName: (ENEMY), s32'CmnActHajikareAir'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(0)
      endIf: 
      ifNot: Mem(ActReg5)
        battleStats: s32'GiveDustCounter', 0, 1
        runOnObject: (ENEMY)
          battleStats: s32'SufferDustCounter', 0, 1
        endRunOnObject: 
        disableWallBreak: 1
        counterDisableWallBreak: 1
        forceWallBreak: 0
        hitStop: 45
        shortHitstop: 0
        disableHitstop: 0
        slowHitstop: 1, 1
        hitAirPushbackX: Val(50000)
        hitAirPushbackY: Val(75000)
        riscConsumeStarter: 5
        setProration: 100
        forcedComboScaleCount: 0
        pushbackX: 200
        groundHitEffect: (TAILSPIN)
        airHitEffect: (TAILSPIN)
        attackFrontDirection: (SELF)
        wallBounceCount: 0
        noGravityScaling: 0
        unburstableTime: 92
        dustInvulnTime: 1
        fuwafuwa: 0
        invulnForce: 1
        slowdownEndOnHit: 1
        hitRedRomanCancelTime: 10
        whiffCancelOptionBufferTime: s32'RomanCancelAttack', 43
        upon: (PLAYER_AFTER_EXECUTE_DAMAGE)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (PLAYER_AFTER_EXECUTE_DAMAGE)
          if: Mem(IsMainPlayerSelf)

postSubroutineBegin: s32'CPUEstimate'
  if: Mem(IsTutorialMode)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(TutorialPhase), Val(3)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(BackWallDistance), Val(250000)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyFrontDistance), Val(500000)
          skillLowEstimation: s32'CmnBAirDash'
          skillLowEstimation: s32'CmnBDash'
          skillLowEstimation: s32'CmnBJump'
          skillLowEstimation: s32'CmnBHighJump'
          skillLowEstimation: s32'CmnVJump'
          skillLowEstimation: s32'CmnVHighJump'
          if: Mem(IsLand)
            ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDistanceY), Val(100000)
              debugLogForScript: s32'player near Y', 0, 0
              skillHighEstimation: s32'CmnFHighJump'
              skillHighEstimation: s32'CmnFAirDash'
            endIf: 
            else: 
              skillHighEstimation: s32'CmnFDash'
            endElse: 
          endIf: 
          else: 
            skillHighEstimation: s32'CmnFAirDash'
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        skillHighEstimation: s32'CmnBWalk'
        skillHighEstimation: s32'CmnBHighJump'
        skillHighEstimation: s32'CmnBAirDash'
        skillLowEstimation: s32'CmnFWalk'
        skillLowEstimation: s32'CmnFDash'
        skillLowEstimation: s32'CmnFJump'
        skillLowEstimation: s32'CmnFHighJump'
        skillLowEstimation: s32'CmnFAirDash'
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(TutorialPhase), Val(5)
      runOnObject: (ENEMY)
        modifyBurstGaugeScaled: 100
      endRunOnObject: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(CPUVal0), Val(0)
        checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActBurst'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          debugLogForScript: s32'burst start', 0, 0
          storeValue: Mem(CPUVal0), Val(1)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(CPUVal0), Val(1)
        checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActBurst'
        ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
          debugLogForScript: s32'burst end', 0, 0
          storeValue: Mem(CPUVal0), Val(2)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(CPUVal0), Val(2)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDistance), Val(350000)
          checkMoveFlag: (ENEMY_IN_HITSTUN)
          if: Mem(Tmp)
            checkMoveFlag: (ENEMY_CAN_BURST)
            if: Mem(Tmp)
              ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(CPUVal1), Val(0)
                upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
                  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(CPUVal1), Val(0)
                    setTutorialButtonGuide: s32'TutorialPhase3Burst'
                    storeValue: Mem(CPUVal1), Val(1)
                    fadeOutStart: 50, 30
                  endIf: 
                  debugLogForScript: s32'world stop start', 0, 0
                  superFreeze: 1, 119, 1, 1
                  checkEnemyInput: (INPUT_BURST_BUTTON)
                  if: Mem(Tmp)
                    debugLogForScript: s32'burst input', 0, 0
                    storeValue: Mem(CPUVal2), Val(1)
                  endIf: 
                  if: Mem(CPUVal2)
                    debugLogForScript: s32'world stop end', 0, 0
                    clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
                    fadeOut: 0
                    setTutorialButtonGuide: s32'TBG_OneBefore'
                  endIf: 
                endUpon: 
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

    storeValue: Mem(CPUVal1), Val(1)

beginSubroutine: s32'OnFrameStep'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnFrameStep'
  ifOperation: (AND), Mem(IsTrainingMode), Mem(IsMainPlayerSelf)
    getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_KYK0', 2, 157
    if: Mem(TrainingValue)
      getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_KYK1', 2, 157
      ifNot: Mem(TrainingValue)
        ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal2)
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(IsRecoverableTypeA), Val(1)
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(300)
            isObjectActive: (STACK2)
            ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
              createObject: s32'Taiden_Effect', (ENEMY_CENTER)
              stackObject: (STACK2), (PREVIOUS)
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(ObjReg5)
    ifOperation: (AND), Mem(IsTrainingMode), Mem(IsMainPlayerSelf)
      if: Mem(IsEnableNormalAttack)
        getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_KYK1', 2, 157
        if: Mem(TrainingValue)
          ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal2)
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(1)
            callSubroutine: s32'DI_MeshSetCheck'
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
        else: 
          if: Mem(PlayerVal2)
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(0)
            callSubroutine: s32'DI_MeshSetCheck'
          endIf: 
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
    if: Mem(PlayerVal1)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(1)
        ifNot: Mem(IsEnemyDamage)
          modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(1)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(1)
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(0)
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(0)
  if: Mem(PlayerDamage)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'HomingJump'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'WorldSideBreak_Master_DS'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'WorldSideBreak_Slave_DS'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'WorldSideBreak_Master_DF'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'WorldSideBreak_Slave_DF'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(IsSomebodysCutSceneOrSelfHide)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActRoundWin'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActLose'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(PlayerVal2)
    isObjectActive: (STACK1)
    ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
      ifNot: Mem(ObjReg6)
        createObject: s32'DKY_floor_aura', (PLAYER)
        stackObject: (STACK1), (PREVIOUS)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifNot: Mem(ObjReg6)
      ifNot: Mem(ObjReg7)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(1)
        createSocketLinkParticle: s32'DKY_stand_aura_loop', (EX_POINT_4), 1
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(0)
      deleteSocketLinkParticle: 
    endElse: 
    walkFSpeed: 8600
    walkBSpeed: 6000
    initDashFSpeed: 20000
    fDashAccelSpeed: 560
  endIf: 
  else: 
    isObjectActive: (STACK1)
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(0)
      deleteSocketLinkParticle: 
      deactivateObjectByName: s32'DKY_floor_aura'
    endIf: 
    walkFSpeed: 6600
    walkBSpeed: 5000
    initDashFSpeed: 15000
    fDashAccelSpeed: 560
  endElse: 
  modifyVar2: (MUL), Mem(HitPointMax), Val(30)
  modifyVar2: (DIV), Mem(Tmp), Val(100)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(HitPoint), Mem(Tmp)
    checkMoveFlag: (REQUIRES_50_TENSION)
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(0)
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(0)
  endElse: 
  if: Mem(IsTo3)
    ifNot: Mem(IsMainPlayerSelf)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(0)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(ObjReg6)
    if: Mem(PlayerVal3)
      ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal2)
        ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal4)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(9)
          createObject: s32'dky_aura', (AURA)
        endIf: 
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(-1)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(0)
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  isObjectActive: (STACK3)
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(1)
    ifTrueInObject: (STACK3), Mem(ActReg0)
      isObjectActive: (STACK4)
      ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(0)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    isObjectActive: (STACK4)
    ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(0)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(1)
    endElse: 
  endElse: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'DI_MeshSetCheck'
  ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal2)
    ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal2), Mem(PlayerVal5)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal5), Mem(PlayerVal2)
      setDefaultMeshSet: s32'Low'
      meshSetClearNameExchange: 
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'High', s32'High'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'nohead', s32'nohead'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'headonly', s32'headonly'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamageLow', s32'CmnCutSceneDamageLow'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamageHigh', s32'CmnCutSceneDamageHigh'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_POT', s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_POT'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_FAU', s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_FAU'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_SLY', s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_SLY'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'NoToge', s32'NoToge'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'MS_1', s32'MS_1'
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal2), Mem(PlayerVal5)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal5), Mem(PlayerVal2)
      setDefaultMeshSet: s32'Low_Di'
      meshSetClearNameExchange: 
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'High', s32'High_DI'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'nohead', s32'nohead_DI'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'headonly', s32'headonly_DI'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamageLow', s32'CmnCutSceneDamageLow_DI'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamageHigh', s32'CmnCutSceneDamageHigh_DI'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_POT', s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_POT_D'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_FAU', s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_FAU_D'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_SLY', s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_SLY_D'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'NoToge', s32'NoToge_DI'

    endIf: 
  endElse:

      playCameraAnimation: s32'kyk800cs', 23, 0, -1
    endIf:

      playCameraAnimation: s32'kyk800cs', 23, 30, -1
    endElse: 
    cinesco: 1
    swapMeshSet: s32'High'
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 2147483647
  upon: (IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(1)
      resetSaturation: 1, 1

      resetDiffusion: 1, 1
      setDiffusionLuminance: -1, 1400, 50
      setDiffusionThreshold: -1, 0, 50

  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_Dust_HomingJump'
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(0)

    storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(0)

    setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 78
    upon: (TIMER)
      upon: (IDLING)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(50)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1000)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1000)
        endIf: 
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(6)
          ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
            spriteBlend: s32'kyk025_02', 2, 45
          endIf: 
          else: 
            spriteBlend: s32'kyk025_02', 2, 45
            ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(6)
              storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
            endIf: 
          endElse: 
        endIf:

    endUpon: 
  endUpon:
